Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Luminary 96, the original release of the Apollo 11 Lunar Module (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software.

The reconstruction began with reconstructed source code for Luminary 97. Changes between revisions 96 and 97 were backed out, as described by anomal report LNY-59. transcribed from a digitized copy of that program. The reconstruction was verified by matching memory-bank checksums to those listed in drawing 2021152D. Note that page numbers in the reconstructed code match those on the Luminary 099 revision 001 printout, although the added code would likely have changed page numbers for a real Luminary 96 listing.

Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. 

020712,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
020713,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
020714,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary revision 96.
020715,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the
020716,000006:                                                                                                  ##              original release of the flight software for the Lunar 
020717,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Module's (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 11.
020718,000008:                                                                                                  ##              The code has been recreated from a previously reconstructed
020719,000009:                                                                                                  ##              copy of Luminary 97 by undoing changes described in anomaly
020720,000010:                                                                                                  ##              report LNY-59. The code has been adapted such that the
020721,000011:                                                                                                  ##              resulting bugger words exactly match those specified for
020722,000012:                                                                                                  ##              Luminary 96 in NASA drawing 2021152D, which gives relatively
020723,000013:                                                                                                  ##              high confidence that the reconstruction is correct.
020724,000014:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 492-613
020725,000015:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
020726,000016:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
020727,000017:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
020728,000018:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2019-08-04 MAS  Created from Luminary 97.

020731,000021:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
020732,000022: 
020733,000023:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
020734,000024: 
020735,000025:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
020736,000026:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
020737,000027: 
020738,000028:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
020739,000029: 
020740,000030:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
020741,000031:                                                                                                  #        STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
020742,000032:                                                                                                  #        THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
020743,000033:                                                                                                  #        ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
020744,000034: 
020745,000035:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
020746,000036: 
020747,000037:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
020748,000038: 
020749,000039:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
020750,000040: 
020751,000041:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      FLAGUP
020752,000042:                                                                                                  #        GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                       FLAGDOWN
020753,000043:                                                                                                  #        R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)                    BANKCALL
020754,000044:                                                                                                  #        LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)                     TASKOVER
020755,000045:                                                                                                  #        LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
020756,000046:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
020757,000047:                                                                                                  #        R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                          ENDOFJOB
020758,000048:                                                                                                  #        R22LEM  (DATA READ)                             GOPERF1
020759,000049:                                                                                                  #        R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)  
020760,000050:                                                                                                  #        PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
020761,000051: 
020762,000052:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
020763,000053: 
020764,000054:                                                                                                  #        P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
020765,000055:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
020766,000056: 
020767,000057:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
020768,000058: 
020769,000059:                                                                                                  #        RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
020770,000060: 
020771,000061:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
020772,000062: 
020773,000063:                                                                                                  #        TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
020774,000064: 
020775,000065:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
020776,000066: 
020777,000067:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
020778,000068: 
020779,000069:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, RNDVZFLG, ACMODFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG,
020780,000070: 
020781,000071:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
020782,000072: 
020783,000073:                                                                                                  #        CENTRALS - A,Q,L
020784,000074: 
020785,000075: 25,2062  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
020786,000076: 
020787,000077: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
020788,000078: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
020789,000079: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
020790,000080: 
020791,000081: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
020792,000082: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20

021200,000490:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021201,000491: 
021202,000492:                                                                                                  #        PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021203,000493:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 3
021204,000494:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021205,000495: 
021206,000496:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021207,000497: 
021208,000498:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021209,000499:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
021210,000500:                                                                                                  #        CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
021211,000501:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
021212,000502: 
021213,000503:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021214,000504: 
021215,000505:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
021216,000506: 
021217,000507:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021218,000508: 
021219,000509:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL                                        FLAGUP

021222,000512:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER                                        FINDVAC

021226,000516:                                                                                                  #        P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021227,000517:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E

021289,000579:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
021290,000580:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021291,000581: 
021292,000582:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021293,000583:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021294,000584: 
021295,000585:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021296,000586: 
021297,000587:                                                                                                  #        TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
021298,000588:                                                                                                  #        LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
021299,000589: 
021300,000590:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021301,000591: 
021302,000592:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021303,000593:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R22LEM
021304,000594: 
021305,000595:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021306,000596: 
021307,000597:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.1         GOFLASH         WAITLIST
021308,000598:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.2         PRIOLARM        BANKCALL
021309,000599:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.3         R61LEM
021310,000600: 
021311,000601:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021312,000602: 
021313,000603:                                                                                                  #        R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE, UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
021314,000604:                                                                                                  #        UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
021315,000605:                                                                                                  #        R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.
021316,000606: 
021317,000607:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021318,000608: 
021319,000609:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM
021320,000610:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 525 LOS NOT WITHIN 3 DEGREE LIMIT
021321,000611: 
021322,000612:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021323,000613: 
021324,000614:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR22.3
021325,000615: 
021326,000616:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021327,000617: 
021328,000618:                                                                                                  #        SEE LSR22.1, LSR22.2, LSR22.3
021329,000619: 
021330,000620:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021331,000621: 
021332,000622:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
021333,000623: 
021334,000624:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021335,000625: 
021336,000626:                                                                                                  #        SEE LSR22.1, LSR22.2, LSR22.3
021337,000627: 
021338,000628: 24,2451  E7,1737                                  EBANK=   LRS22.1X                              
021339,000629: 24,2451                                           COUNT*   $$/R22                                
021340,000630: 24,2451           05353        R22LEM             TC       PHASCHNG

021504,000794:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
021505,000795:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021506,000796: 
021507,000797:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021508,000798:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021509,000799: 
021510,000800:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021511,000801: 
021512,000802:                                                                                                  #        TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
021513,000803:                                                                                                  #        OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR.  ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
021514,000804: 
021515,000805:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021516,000806: 
021517,000807:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021518,000808:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R21LEM
021519,000809: 
021520,000810:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021521,000811: 
021522,000812:                                                                                                  #        FINDVAC         FLAGUP          ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
021523,000813:                                                                                                  #        NOVAC           INTPRET         LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
021524,000814:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        JOBSLEEP        JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
021525,000815:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER        BANKCALL        RADSTALL        RRDESSM
021526,000816: 
021527,000817:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
021528,000818:                                                                                                  #        
021529,000819:                                                                                                  #        WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED, BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
021530,000820:                                                                                                  #        WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER (BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
021531,000821: 
021532,000822:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021533,000823: 
021534,000824:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
021535,000825:                                                                                                  #        THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
021536,000826:                                                                                                  #        ACQUISITION
021537,000827: 
021538,000828:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021539,000829: 
021540,000830:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
021541,000831: 
021542,000832:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021543,000833: 
021544,000834:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
021545,000835: 
021546,000836:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021547,000837: 
021548,000838:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        LOKONSW
021549,000839: 
021550,000840:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021551,000841: 
021552,000842:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
021553,000843: 
021554,000844: 24,2674  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021555,000845: 24,2674                                           COUNT*   $$/R21

021736,001026:

021813,001103:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
021814,001104:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021815,001105: 
021816,001106:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021817,001107:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021818,001108: 
021819,001109:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021820,001110: 
021821,001111:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
021822,001112:                                                                                                  #        FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
021823,001113:                                                                                                  #        THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
021824,001114: 
021825,001115:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
021826,001116: 
021827,001117:                                                                                                  #        CAF     PRIONN
021828,001118:                                                                                                  #        TC      FINDVAC
021829,001119:                                                                                                  #        EBANK=  DATAGOOD
021830,001120:                                                                                                  #        2CADR   R24LEM
021831,001121: 
021832,001122:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021833,001123: 
021834,001124:                                                                                                  #        FLAGUP          FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
021835,001125:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM          GOFLASHR        FINDVAC
021836,001126:                                                                                                  #        ENDOFJOB        NOVAC           LSR24.1
021837,001127: 
021838,001128:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021839,001129: 
021840,001130:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.  HE CAN EITHER
021841,001131:                                                                                                  #        REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
021842,001132:                                                                                                  #        PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
021843,001133: 
021844,001134:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021845,001135: 
021846,001136:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
021847,001137: 
021848,001138:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
021849,001139: 
021850,001140:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
021851,001141: 
021852,001142:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021853,001143: 
021854,001144:                                                                                                  #        SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
021855,001145: 
021856,001146:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021857,001147: 
021858,001148:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, ACMODFLG
021859,001149: 
021860,001150: 24,3206  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD

021864,001154: 24,3210           05516                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
021865,001155: 24,3211           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
021866,001156: 24,3212           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO

021929,001219:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
021930,001220:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021931,001221: 
021932,001222:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO: 3               DATE: 4-11-67
021933,001223:                                                                                                  #        MOD BY: P VOLANTE   SDC
021934,001224: 
021935,001225:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION -
021936,001226: 
021937,001227:                                                                                                  #        TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO ENABLE RR
021938,001228:                                                                                                  #        TRACKING OF THE CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED
021939,001229:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE.
021940,001230: 
021941,001231:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021942,001232: 
021943,001233:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021944,001234:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R61LEM
021945,001235: 
021946,001236:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021947,001237: 
021948,001238:                                                                                                  #        LPS20.1         VECPOINT
021949,001239:                                                                                                  #        KALCMAN3
021950,001240: 
021951,001241:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021952,001242: 
021953,001243:                                                                                                  #        NORMAL RETURN IS TO CALLER + 1
021954,001244: 
021955,001245:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021956,001246: 
021957,001247:                                                                                                  #        TERMINATE P20 + R61 BY BRANCHING TO P20END IF BOTH TRACKFLAG +
021958,001248:                                                                                                  #        RENDEZVOUS FLAG ARE NOT SET.

022138,001428:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ RRLIMCHK                                                        ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
022139,001429: 
022140,001430:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022141,001431: 
022142,001432:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022143,001433:                                                                                                  #        THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.  INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022144,001434:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2.  THE CURRENT RR
022145,001435:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022146,001436:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022147,001437: 
022148,001438:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022149,001439:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022150,001440:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022151,001441:                                                                                                  #        IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022152,001442: 
022153,001443:                                                                                                  #        MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022154,001444:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN
022155,001445:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022156,001446:                                                                                                  #        AND -125 (+235) DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022157,001447:                                                                                                  #        TO L +3.
022158,001448: 
022159,001449:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022160,001450: 
022161,001451:                                                                                                  #        L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022162,001452:                                                                                                  #        L  +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022163,001453: 
022164,001454:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022165,001455: 
022166,001456:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022167,001457:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022168,001458:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT EBANK).
022169,001459: 
022170,001460:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_   MAGSUB
022171,001461: 
022172,001462:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022173,001463: 
022174,001464:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022175,001465: 
022176,001466:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         L + 2   (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022177,001467:                                                                                                  #                L + 3   (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022178,001468:

022222,001512:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ SETTRKF                                                         . IF EITHER:
022223,001513: 
022224,001514:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022225,001515:                                                                                                  #        SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
022226,001516:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022227,001517:                                                                                                  #        IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022228,001518:                                                                                                  #        IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
022229,001519:                                                                                                  #                1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022230,001520:                                                                                                  #                   AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022231,001521:                                                                                                  #                2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022232,001522:                                                                                                  #                   8,5)
022233,001523:                                                                                                  #                3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022234,001524:                                                                                                  #        THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022235,001525:                                                                                                  #        IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022236,001526:                                                                                                  #        LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
022237,001527:                                                                                                  #        THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
022238,001528:                                                                                                  #        TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
022239,001529:                                                                                                  #                A) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
022240,001530:                                                                                                  #                B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022241,001531:                                                                                                  #                   EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022242,001532:                                                                                                  #                C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022243,001533:                                                                                                  #                   WITH EITHER THE AL
022244,001534:

022246,001536:

022248,001538:

022250,001540: 
022251,001541:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  NONE
022252,001542: 
022253,001543:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022254,001544: 
022255,001545:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL LAMP

022294,001584:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
022295,001585: 
022296,001586:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022297,001587: 
022298,001588:                                                                                                  #        RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
022299,001589:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022300,001590:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022301,001591:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE.  UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022302,001592:                                                                                                  #        WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022303,001593:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
022304,001594:                                                                                                  #        INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022305,001595:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7).  IF
022306,001596:                                                                                                  #        SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022307,001597:                                                                                                  #        FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022308,001598:                                                                                                  #        RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM.  IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022309,001599:                                                                                                  #        TO TASKOVER.
022310,001600: 
022311,001601:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
022312,001602:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
022313,001603:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022314,001604: 
022315,001605:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022316,001606: 
022317,001607:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, STATE
022318,001608: 
022319,001609:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR

022324,001614: 
022325,001615:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)

022343,001633:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
022344,001634: 
022345,001635:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022346,001636:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
022347,001637:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022348,001638:                                                                                                  #        LAMP IF REQUIRED.  INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022349,001639:                                                                                                  #        BIT 1) IS SET.  FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022350,001640:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
022351,001641:                                                                                                  #        WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022352,001642:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
022353,001643:                                                                                                  #        TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES.  THE
022354,001644:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED.  THE
022355,001645:                                                                                                  #        CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022356,001646:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES.  IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022357,001647:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022358,001648:                                                                                                  #        IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022359,001649:                                                                                                  #        INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1.  SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022360,001650:                                                                                                  #        SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022361,001651: 
022362,001652:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  L  TC  RRZEROSB  (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
022363,001653: 
022364,001654:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022365,001655: 
022366,001656:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
022367,001657: 
022368,001658:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
022369,001659: 
022370,001660:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022371,001661: 
022372,001662:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022373,001663: 
022374,001664:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
022375,001665: 
022376,001666:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
022377,001667:

022381,001671: 25,2074           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.
022382,001672: 25,2075           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                #  TURN ON ZERO RR CDU

022419,001709:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
022420,001710: 
022421,001711:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022422,001712: 
022423,001713:                                                                                                  #        DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022424,001714:                                                                                                  #        TO A SAFE POSITION.  INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022425,001715:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022426,001716:                                                                                                  #        AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022427,001717:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS.  THE RR
022428,001718:                                                                                                  #        TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022429,001719:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING.  IN EITHER
022430,001720:                                                                                                  #        CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022431,001721:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12).  RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022432,001722:                                                                                                  #        TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022433,001723:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022434,001724:                                                                                                  #        MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED.  RRSONLY IS THEN
022435,001725:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022436,001726:                                                                                                  #        -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022437,001727:                                                                                                  #        REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022438,001728:                                                                                                  #        FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
022439,001729:                                                                                                  #        REPOSRPT.  HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
022440,001730:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022441,001731:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10).  IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES.  IF NOT PRESENT
022442,001732:                                                                                                  #        INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022443,001733:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022444,001734:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER.
022445,001735: 
022446,001736:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022447,001737: 
022448,001738:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022449,001739:                                                                                                  #        NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022450,001740: 
022451,001741:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022452,001742: 
022453,001743:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022454,001744: 
022455,001745:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022456,001746: 
022457,001747:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
022458,001748: 
022459,001749:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022460,001750: 
022461,001751:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022462,001752:

022464,001754:

022512,001802:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                         IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
022513,001803: 
022514,001804:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
022515,001805:                                                                                                  #        REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE.  IT DRIVES THE
022516,001806:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
022517,001807:                                                                                                  #        180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
022518,001808:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
022519,001809:                                                                                                  #        TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
022520,001810:                                                                                                  #        INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL.  ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
022521,001811:                                                                                                  #        AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS).  INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022522,001812:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED.  CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
022523,001813:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
022524,001814:                                                                                                  #        OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
022525,001815:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022526,001816:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN.  CONTROL IS AGAIN
022527,001817:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
022528,001818:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
022529,001819:                                                                                                  #        -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1.  RMODINV
022530,001820:                                                                                                  #        IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
022531,001821:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE.  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
022532,001822:                                                                                                  #        IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE.  THE PROGRAM
022533,001823:                                                                                                  #        THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
022534,001824: 
022535,001825:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022536,001826: 
022537,001827:                                                                                                  #        FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
022538,001828:                                                                                                  #        THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
022539,001829:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
022540,001830:                                                                                                  #        OTHER MODE.
022541,001831: 
022542,001832:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022543,001833:

022609,001899:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_        RRTONLY, RRSONLY
022610,001900: 
022611,001901:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022612,001902: 
022613,001903:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
022614,001904:                                                                                                  #        RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION.  IT DRIVES TO
022615,001905:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
022616,001906:                                                                                                  #        FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED.  IF BOTH EXIST,
022617,001907:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS).  THIS INDICATES
022618,001908:                                                                                                  #        THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
022619,001909:                                                                                                  #        WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
022620,001910:                                                                                                  #        REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11).  IF NONE
022621,001911:                                                                                                  #        OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
022622,001912:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  IF YES,
022623,001913:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS
022624,001914:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
022625,001915:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE SET = 0.  FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
022626,001916:                                                                                                  #        REPEATED.
022627,001917: 
022628,001918:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     L-1     CAF     *ANGLE*         (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
022629,001919:                                                                                                  #                        L       TC      RRTONLY         (TRUNNION ONLY)
022630,001920:                                                                                                  #                        RRSONLY                         (SHAFT ONLY)
022631,001921:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
022632,001922:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
022633,001923: 
022634,001924:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022635,001925: 
022636,001926:                                                                                                  #        C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
022637,001927:

022639,001929:

022643,001933:

022702,001992:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                          RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
022703,001993: 
022704,001994:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022705,001995: 
022706,001996:                                                                                                  #        RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
022707,001997:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTER SCALING.  RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
022708,001998:                                                                                                  #        GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
022709,001999:                                                                                                  #        TO THE DESIRED VALUES.  INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
022710,002000:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
022711,002001:                                                                                                  #        384 PULSES.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
022712,002002:                                                                                                  #        LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES.  THE DIFFERENCE IS
022713,002003:                                                                                                  #        THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
022714,002004:                                                                                                  #        THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
022715,002005:                                                                                                  #        THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
022716,002006:                                                                                                  #        PASS).  FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
022717,002007:                                                                                                  #        OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
022718,002008:                                                                                                  #        ARE SET.  THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
022719,002009: 
022720,002010:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022721,002011:                                                                                                  #

022723,002013:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES

022812,002102:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                        R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
022813,002103: 
022814,002104:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022815,002105: 
022816,002106:                                                                                                  #        THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
022817,002107:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
022818,002108:                                                                                                  #        (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
022819,002109:                                                                                                  #        ORIENTATION.  INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
022820,002110:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
022821,002111:                                                                                                  #        MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
022822,002112:                                                                                                  #        RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
022823,002113:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
022824,002114:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
022825,002115:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
022826,002116:                                                                                                  #        LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
022827,002117:                                                                                                  #        REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
022828,002118:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED.  FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
022829,002119:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
022830,002120:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
022831,002121:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS.  IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
022832,002122:                                                                                                  #        THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
022833,002123:                                                                                                  #        INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
022834,002124:                                                                                                  #        EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
022835,002125:                                                                                                  #        OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
022836,002126:                                                                                                  #        BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
022837,002127:                                                                                                  #        TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
022838,002128: 
022839,002129:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022840,002130: 
022841,002131:                                                                                                  #        L       STCALL  RRTARGET        (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
022842,002132:                                                                                                  #        L+1     RRDESSM
022843,002133:                                                                                                  #        L+2     BASIC                   (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
022844,002134:                                                                                                  #        L+3     BASIC                   (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
022845,002135: 
022846,002136:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022847,002137: 
022848,002138:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES

022853,002143:                                                                                                  #        PART OF), RMODINV

022902,002192:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                       STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
022903,002193: 
022904,002194:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
022905,002195:                                                                                                  #        STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
022906,002196:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
022907,002197:                                                                                                  #        AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
022908,002198:                                                                                                  #        OPERATION.  IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
022909,002199:                                                                                                  #        ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
022910,002200:                                                                                                  #        OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
022911,002201:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATION BEGINS.  INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
022912,002202:                                                                                                  #        THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
022913,002203:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5).  BIT 10
022914,002204:                                                                                                  #        OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
022915,002205:                                                                                                  #        THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF SET,
022916,002206:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
022917,002207:                                                                                                  #        AND RRDESNB).  THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
022918,002208:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
022919,002209:                                                                                                  #        REQUESTED.  IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
022920,002210:                                                                                                  #        WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
022921,002211:                                                                                                  #        AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
022922,002212:                                                                                                  #        DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
022923,002213:                                                                                                  #        COUNTERS.  A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
022924,002214:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
022925,002215: 
022926,002216:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
