Page 545 

023075,002365:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
023076,002366: 
023077,002367:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023078,002368: 
023079,002369:                                                                                                  #        BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
023080,002370:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION.  INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
023081,002371:                                                                                                  #        REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS.  IF SO,
023082,002372:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
023083,002373:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTED.  IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
023084,002374:                                                                                                  #        FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF
023085,002375:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
023086,002376:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND.  IF THE REPOSITION
023087,002377:                                                                                                  #        FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023088,002378:                                                                                                  #        BIT 15) IS CHECKED.  IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
023089,002379:                                                                                                  #        MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
023090,002380:                                                                                                  #        REPEATING AT STDESIG.  IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
023091,002381:                                                                                                  #        TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
023092,002382:                                                                                                  #        IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023093,002383:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
023094,002384:                                                                                                  #        CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.  IF DESIGNATE
023095,002385:                                                                                                  #        IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
023096,002386:                                                                                                  #        EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
023097,002387:                                                                                                  #        SIGNAL.  IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
023098,002388:                                                                                                  #        RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
023099,002389:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
023100,002390:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND.  IF
023101,002391:                                                                                                  #        TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
023102,002392:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
023103,002393:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
023104,002394: 
023105,002395:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023106,002396: 
023107,002397:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
023108,002398:                                                                                                  #        TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
023109,002399:                                                                                                  #        TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
023110,002400: 
023111,002401:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023112,002402:                                                                                                  #        DESCOUNT, RADMODES
023113,002403: 
023114,002404:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023115,002405:                                                                                                  #        ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
023116,002406: 
023117,002407:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
023118,002408: 
023119,002409:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
023120,002410:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
023121,002411: 
023122,002412:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
023123,002413:                                                                                                  #                ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
023124,002414:                                                                                                  #                RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
023125,002415: 
023126,002416: 25,2573           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

023170,002460:

Page 547 

023172,002462:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
023173,002463: 
023174,002464:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023175,002465: 
023176,002466:                                                                                                  #        DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
023177,002467:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS.  INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
023178,002468:                                                                                                  #        THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
023179,002469:                                                                                                  #        NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY.  THE
023180,002470:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
023181,002471:                                                                                                  #                + SHAFT = LOS . (COS(S), 0, -SIN(S))  (DOT PRODUCT)
023182,002472:                                                                                                  #                - TRUNNION = LOS . (SIN(T)SIN(S), COS(T), SIN(T)COS(S))
023183,002473:                                                                                                  #        THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
023184,002474:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
023185,002475:                                                                                                  #        POLARITY OF THE COMMAND.  AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
023186,002476:                                                                                                  #        SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
023187,002477:                                                                                                  #        .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
023188,002478:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
023189,002479:                                                                                                  #        THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
023190,002480:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
023191,002481:                                                                                                  #        IS IN PROGRESS.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
023192,002482:                                                                                                  #        OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED.  IF NO
023193,002483:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
023194,002484:                                                                                                  #        INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
023195,002485:                                                                                                  #        CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023196,002486:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
023197,002487:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
023198,002488:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
023199,002489:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
023200,002490:                                                                                                  #        PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
023201,002491:                                                                                                  #        LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE
023202,002492:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
023203,002493:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
023204,002494:                                                                                                  #        CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
023205,002495:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
023206,002496:                                                                                                  #        RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL.  IF RR DATA GOOD
023207,002497:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
023208,002498:                                                                                                  #        THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
023209,002499:                                                                                                  #        AND ENDOFJOB CALLED.  IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
023210,002500:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023211,002501:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
023212,002502:                                                                                                  #        VIA ENDOFJOB.
023213,002503: 
023214,002504:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023215,002505: 
023216,002506:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
023217,002507: 
023218,002508:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023219,002509: 
023220,002510:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
023221,002511:                                                                                                  #        LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
023222,002512: 
023223,002513:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023224,002514: 
023225,002515:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT

Page 548 

023227,002517: 
023228,002518:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023229,002519: 
023230,002520:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023231,002521: 
023232,002522:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023233,002523: 
023234,002524:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  ENDOFJOB (ALWAYS)
023235,002525: 
023236,002526: 25,2636           00006        DODES              EXTEND                                         
023237,002527: 25,2637           30036                           DCA      CDUT                                  
023238,002528: 25,2640           53110                           DXCH     TANG

023841,003131:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  LPS20.1 VECTOR EXTRAPOLATION AND LOS COMPUTATION
023842,003132:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO. 2    BY J.D. COYNE   SDC     DATE 12-7-66
023843,003133: 
023844,003134:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023845,003135:                                                                                                  #        1)      EXTRAPOLATE THE LEM AND CSM VECTORS IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE TIME REFERED TO IN CALLER + 1.
023846,003136:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPUTES THE LOS VECTOR TO THE CSM, CONVERTS IT TO STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES AND STORES IT IN RRTARGET.
023847,003137:                                                                                                  #        3)      COMPUTES THE MAGNITUDE OF THE LOS VECTOR AND STORES IT IN MLOSV
023848,003138: 
023849,003139:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE      CALL
023850,003140:                                                                                                  #                                LPS20.1
023851,003141: 
023852,003142:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023853,003143:                                                                                                  #        LEMPREC, CSMPREC
023854,003144: 
023855,003145:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT_  RETURN TO CALLER + 2
023856,003146: 
023857,003147:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS_  NONE
023858,003148: 
023859,003149:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023860,003150: 
023861,003151:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT_
023862,003152:                                                                                                  #        LOS VECTOR (HALF UNIT) IN SM COORDINATES STORED IN RRTARGET
023863,003153:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF THE LOS VECTOR (METERS SCALED B-29) STORED IN MSLOV
023864,003154:                                                                                                  #        RRNBSW CLEARED
023865,003155: 
023866,003156:                                                                                                  #  INITIALIZED ERASEABLE
023867,003157:                                                                                                  #        TDEC1 MUST CONTAIN THE TIME FOR EXTRAPOLATION
023868,003158:                                                                                                  #        SEE ORBITAL INTEGRATION ROUTINE
023869,003159: 
023870,003160:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS_
023871,003161:                                                                                                  #        MPAC DESTROYED BY THIS ROUTINE
023872,003162: 
023873,003163: 23,2314                                           BANK     23                                    
023874,003164: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
023875,003165: 24,2000                                           BANK

Page 565 

023877,003167: 24,3255                                           COUNT*   $$/LPS20                              
023878,003168: 
023879,003169: 24,3255           43020        LPS20.1            STQ      BOFF                                  
023880,003170: 24,3256           01757                                    LS21X                                 
023881,003171: 24,3257           01343                                    LOSCMFLG                              #  LOSCMFLG = 0 MEANS NOT CALLED BY R21
023882,003172: 24,3260           51264                                    LMINT                                 #  SO CALL LEMCONIC TO GET LM STATE
023883,003173: 24,3261           77614                           BON                                            #  IF IN R21 AND ON LUNAR SURFACE
023884,003174: 24,3262           04307                                    SURFFLAG                              #  DON'T CALL LEMCONIC
023885,003175: 24,3263           51274                                    CSMINT                                
023886,003176: 24,3264           77624        LMINT              CALL                                           
023887,003177: 24,3265           27100                                    LEMCONIC                              #  EXTRAPOLATE LEM
023888,003178: 24,3266           77775                           VLOAD                                          
023889,003179: 24,3267           00001                                    RATT                                  
023890,003180: 24,3270           26352                           STOVL    LMPOS                                 #  SAVE LM POSITION B-29
023891,003181: 24,3271           00007                                    VATT                                  
023892,003182: 24,3272           16360                           STODL    LMVEL                                 #  SAVE LM VELOCITY B-7
023893,003183: 24,3273           00015                                    TAT                                   
023894,003184: 24,3274           34041        CSMINT             STCALL   TDEC1                                 
023895,003185: 24,3275           27066                                    CSMCONIC                              #  EXTRAPOLATE CSM
023896,003186: 24,3276           52375                           VLOAD    VSU                                   #  COMPUTE RELATIVE VELOCITY V(CSM) - V(LM)
023897,003187: 24,3277           00007                                    VATT                                  
023898,003188: 24,3300           02360                                    LMVEL                                 
023899,003189: 24,3301           76521                           MXV      VSL1

023970,003260:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
023971,003261:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1           BY: P. VOLANTE  SDC             DATE:  11-15-66
023972,003262: 
023973,003263:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023974,003264:                                                                                                  #        1)      READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE, TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES, THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME.  CONVERTS THIS
023975,003265:                                                                                                  #                DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3).  CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE, FOR
023976,003266:                                                                                                  #                RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
023977,003267:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
023978,003268: 
023979,003269:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
023980,003270: 
023981,003271:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
023982,003272:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          LPS20.1
023983,003273:                                                                                                  #        RRRANGE         BANKCALL
023984,003274:                                                                                                  #        RADSTALL        CDULOGIC
023985,003275:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            SMNB
023986,003276: 
023987,003277:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
023988,003278: 
023989,003279:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
023990,003280:                                                                                                  #        00001 - ERROR EXIT 1 - RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
023991,003281:                                                                                                  #        00002 - ERROR EXIT 2 - RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
023992,003282: 
023993,003283:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521 - COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
023994,003284:                                                                                                  #        (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
023995,003285: 
023996,003286:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  RRLOSVEC - THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR (USED BY LRS22.2) - A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
023997,003287:                                                                                                  #        RM - THE RR RANGE READING (TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29 (USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
023998,003288: 
023999,003289:                                                                                                  #        ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
024000,003290:                                                                                                  #                RDOTM - THE RR RANGE-RATE READING, DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
024001,003291:                                                                                                  #                RRTRUN - RR TRUNION ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024002,003292:                                                                                                  #                RRSHAFT - RR SHAFT ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024003,003293:                                                                                                  #                AIG,AMG,AOG - THE CDU ANGLES, THREE SP WORDS

024194,003484:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                DATE - 29 MAY 1967
024195,003485:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                             LOG SECTION - P20-25
024196,003486:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                    ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
024197,003487: 
024198,003488:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024199,003489:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
024200,003490:                                                                                                  #        RADAR.  (RANGE, RANGE RATE, SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES).  THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
024201,003491:                                                                                                  #        WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
024202,003492: 
024203,003493:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
024204,003494:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER ONLY.  THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
024205,003495:                                                                                                  #        R22 LEM ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA.  IF THE
024206,003496:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED.  THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM TO DISPLAY
024207,003497:                                                                                                  #        THE DEVIATIONS.  IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM RETURNS TO LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
024208,003498:                                                                                                  #        DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR.  IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
024209,003499:                                                                                                  #        PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK, I.E.,  R22LEM GETS THE NEXT MARK.
024210,003500: 
024211,003501:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024212,003502:                                                                                                  #        WLINIT          LGCUPDTE        INTEGRV         INCORP1         ARCTAN
024213,003503:                                                                                                  #        GETULC          RARARANG        INCORP2         NBSM            INTSTALL
024214,003504: 
024215,003505:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024216,003506:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024217,003507:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
024218,003508:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
024219,003509:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024220,003510:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024221,003511: 
024222,003512:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
024223,003513:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024224,003514:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024225,003515:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024226,003516:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024227,003517:                                                                                                  #                RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
024228,003518:                                                                                                  #                SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS. B0
024229,003519:                                                                                                  #                TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
024230,003520:                                                                                                  #        GIMBAL ANGLES   INNER IN AIG
024231,003521:                                                                                                  #                        MIDDLE IN AMG
024232,003522:                                                                                                  #                        OUTER IN AOG
024233,003523:                                                                                                  #        REFSMMAT
024234,003524:                                                                                                  #        RENDWFLG
024235,003525:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
024236,003526:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
024237,003527: 
024238,003528:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
024239,003529:                                                                                                  #        PUSHLIST -- ALL
024240,003530:                                                                                                  #        MX, MY, MZ (VECTORS)

024242,003532:                                                                                                  #        ULC, RXZ, SINTHETA, LGRET, RDRET, BVECTOR, W.IND, X78T

024635,003925: 
024636,003926:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024637,003927:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
024638,003928:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTER ONLY.  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
024639,003929:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
024640,003930: 
024641,003931:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024642,003932:                                                                                                  #        INSTALL         LGCUPDTE        INCORP1         RP-TO-R
024643,003933:                                                                                                  #        INTEGRV         GETULC          INCORP2
024644,003934: 
024645,003935:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024646,003936:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024647,003937:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR

Page 583 

024649,003939:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22 DISP METERS B-29
024650,003940:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024651,003941:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024652,003942: 
024653,003943:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
024654,003944:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024655,003945:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024656,003946:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024657,003947:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024658,003948:                                                                                                  #        RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
024659,003949:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
024660,003950:

024765,004055: 
024766,004056:                                                                                                  #  GETULC
024767,004057: 
024768,004058:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES THE RELATIVE POSITION VECTOR BETWEEN THE CSM

024795,004085:                                                                                                  #  RADARANG
024796,004086: 
024797,004087:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES SINTHETA = -ULC DOT MY

024859,004149:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1          RR SEARCH ROUTINE
024860,004150:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO 0                      BY P VOLANTE   SDC              DATE 1-15-67
024861,004151: 
024862,004152:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024863,004153: 
024864,004154:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
024865,004155:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
024866,004156:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS.  IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
024867,004157:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
024868,004158: 
024869,004159:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
024870,004160: 
024871,004161:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024872,004162: 
024873,004163:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC        R61LEM
024874,004164:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC        RRDESSM
024875,004165:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY        FLAGDOWN
024876,004166:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        FLAGUP
024877,004167:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            BANKCALL
024878,004168: 
024879,004169:                                                                                                  #  EXIT - TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
024880,004170:

024882,004172: 
024883,004173:                                                                                                  #        DATAGOOD (SP) - FOR DISPLAY IN R1 -     00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
024884,004174:                                                                                                  #                                                11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED

024888,004178:

025112,004402:

Page 594 

025114,004404:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29     (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
025115,004405:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2     BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968.
025116,004406: 
025117,004407:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025118,004408: 
025119,004409:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTED LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
025120,004410:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
025121,004411:                                                                                                  #        THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
025122,004412:                                                                                                  #        THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
025123,004413:                                                                                                  #        DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
025124,004414:                                                                                                  #        INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
025125,004415: 
025126,004416:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
025127,004417: 
025128,004418:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025129,004419: 
025130,004420:                                                                                                  #        REMODE          RRTONLY
025131,004421:                                                                                                  #        UNIT            MPACVBUF
025132,004422:                                                                                                  #        QUICTRIG        AX*SR*T
025133,004423:                                                                                                  #        SPSIN           SPCOS
025134,004424:                                                                                                  #        SETRRECR        RROUT
025135,004425:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          RRRANGE
025136,004426: 
025137,004427:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.
025138,004428: 
025139,004429:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  (ALL FOR DOWNLINK)
025140,004430: 
025141,004431:                                                                                                  #        RM              RDOTM           (RAW)
025142,004432:                                                                                                  #        AIG             AMG             
025143,004433:                                                                                                  #        AOG             TRKMKCNT        TRKMKCNT = 00001 IF SET IS CONSISTENT,
025144,004434:                                                                                                  #        TANGNB          TANGNB +1       OTHERWISE TRKMKCNT = 00000.
025145,004435:                                                                                                  #        MKTIME

Page 595 

025147,004437: 
025148,004438:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025149,004439: 
025150,004440:                                                                                                  #        NOR29FLG        READRFLG                (TO 1 AND 0 BY FRESH START) (RESET NOR29FLG TO LET SERVICER RUN R29)
025151,004441:                                                                                                  #        PIPTIME         RADMODES (BIT 10)       (BIT SET TO 0 BY FRESH START)
025152,004442:                                                                                                  #        R(CSM)          V(CSM)
025153,004443:                                                                                                  #        R               V                       (PIPTIME THRU V BY AVE G IN SERVICER)
025154,004444: 
025155,004445:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
025156,004446: 
025157,004447:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 10)

Page 600 

025344,004634:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
025345,004635: 
025346,004636:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
025347,004637:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
025348,004638:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
025349,004639:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
025350,004640:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
025351,004641: 
025352,004642:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
025353,004643:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
025354,004644: 
025355,004645: 32,2547                                           BANK     32                                    
025356,004646: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
025357,004647: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
025358,004648: 
025359,004649: 32,2547                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
025360,004650: 32,2547  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
025361,004651: 
025362,004652: 32,2547           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
025363,004653: 32,2550           55107                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
025364,004654: 32,2551           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
025365,004655: 
025366,004656: 32,2552           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWOS IN VECTOR LOOP.
025367,004657: 32,2553           54002                           TS       Q                                     
025368,004658: 32,2554           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
025369,004659: 32,2555           12563                           TCF      R29DPAS1                              #  DO THIS ON 1ST PASS THRU LOOP.
025370,004660: 
025371,004661: 32,2556           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (A "PASS" HERE MEANS 3 TIMES AROUND).
025372,004662: 32,2557           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025373,004663: 32,2560           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025374,004664: 32,2561           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025375,004665: 32,2562           21102                           DAS      LOSSM                                 #  ADVANCE LOS VECTOR 1/2 SECOND.
025376,004666: 
025377,004667: 32,2563           00006        R29DPAS1           EXTEND                                         
025378,004668: 32,2564           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025379,004669: 32,2565           31102                           DCA      LOSSM                                 
025380,004670: 32,2566           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     #  MOVE CURRENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR LOS PRO-
025381,004671: 32,2567           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         #  JECTED 1/2 SEC AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025382,004672: 32,2570           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
025383,004673: 32,2571           12577                           TCF      R29DVEND                              #  BUG OUT HERE IN 1ST PASS.
025384,004674: 
025385,004675: 32,2572           00006                           EXTEND                                         
025386,004676: 32,2573           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025387,004677: 32,2574           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025388,004678: 32,2575           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025389,004679: 32,2576           20156                           DAS      MPAC       +1                         #  PROJECT LOS 1 SECOND AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025390,004680: 
025391,004681: 32,2577           10002        R29DVEND           CCS      Q                                     
025392,004682: 32,2600           12552                           TCF      R29DVBEG                              #  BRANCH TO CONTINUE VECTOR LOOP.
025393,004683:

Page 601 

025395,004685:                                                                                                  #  UNITIZE AND TRANSFORM TO NAV BASE AXES THE PRESENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR THE 1-SEC PROJECTED LOS (2ND PASS).
025396,004686: 
025397,004687: 32,2601           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1

025404,004694:

Page 602

025431,004721:                                                                                                  #  THE COSINE IS APPROXIMATELY COS(.5 DEG) OR GREATER (I.E. SMALLER ANGLE).
